162→    return included, skipped\n   163→\n   164→\n   165→def _safe_parse(file_path: Path) -> ast.Module | None:\n   166→    \"\"\"Parse a Python file, returning None on SyntaxError (R2 mitigation).\"\"\"\n   167→    try:\n   168→        source = file_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   169→        return ast.parse(source, filename=str(file_path))\n   170→    except SyntaxError as exc:\n   171→        logger.warning(\"SyntaxError parsing %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n   172→        return None\n   173→    except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as exc:\n   174→        logger.warning(\"Cannot read %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n   175→        return None\n   176→\n   177→\n   178→def _apply_whitelist(\n   179→    findings: list[WiringFinding],\n   180→    whitelist: list[WhitelistEntry],\n   181→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   182→    \"\"\"Mark findings as suppressed if they match a whitelist entry.\"\"\"\n   183→    suppressed_symbols = {\n   184→        (e.symbol, e.finding_type) for e in whitelist\n   185→    }\n   186→    for finding in findings:\n   187→        if (finding.symbol_name, finding.finding_type) in suppressed_symbols:\n   188→            finding.suppressed = True\n   189→            finding.severity = \"info\"\n   190→    return findings\n   191→\n   192→\n   193→# --- G-001: Unwired Callable Analysis (section 5.2.1) ---\n   194→\n   195→\n   196→def _extract_injectable_params(\n   197→    tree: ast.Module, file_path: str\n   198→) -> list[tuple[str, str, int]]:\n   199→    \"\"\"Extract Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n   200→\n   201→    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n   202→    \"\"\"\n   203→    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n   204→\n   205→    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   206→        if not isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n   207→            continue\n   208→\n   209→        for item in node.body:\n   210→            if not isinstance(item, ast.FunctionDef) or item.name != \"__init__\":\n   211→                continue\n   212→\n   213→            for arg in item.args.args:\n   214→                if arg.arg == \"self\":\n   215→                    continue\n   216→                annotation = arg.annotation\n   217→                if annotation is None:\n   218→                    continue\n   219→\n   220→                # Check for Optional[Callable] or Callable | None\n   221→                if _is_optional_callable(annotation):\n   222→                    # Verify default is None\n   223→                    if _has_none_default(item, arg):\n   224→                        symbol = f\"{node.name}.{arg.arg}\"\n   225→                        injectables.append(\n   226→                            (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n   227→                        )\n   228→\n   229→    return injectables\n   230→\n   231→\n   232→def _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n   233→    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n   234→    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n   235→    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n   236→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n   237→            slice_val = annotation.slice\n   238→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   239→                return True\n   240→            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n   241→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n   242→                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n   243→                    return True\n   244→        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n   245→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n   246→            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n   247→                slice_val = annotation.slice\n   248→                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   249→                    return True\n   250→\n   251→    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n   252→    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n   253→        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n   254→        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n   255→                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n   256→            return True\n   257→        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n   258→                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n   259→            return True\n   260→\n   261→    return False\n   262→\n   263→\n   264→def _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n   265→    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n   266→    args = func_def.args\n   267→    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n   268→    all_args = args.args\n   269→    defaults = args.defaults\n   270→\n   271→    if not defaults:\n   272→        return False\n   273→\n   274→    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n   275→    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n   276→    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n   277→        if arg is target_arg:\n   278→            default_idx = i - offset\n   279→            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n   280→                default = defaults[default_idx]\n   281→                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n   282→    return False\n   283→\n   284→\n   285→def _find_wiring_call_sites(\n   286→    param_name: str,\n   287→    class_name: str,\n   288→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n   289→) -> bool:\n   290→    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n   291→    for tree in trees.values():\n   292→        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   293→            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n   294→                # Check keyword arguments\n   295→                for kw in node.keywords:\n   296→                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n   297→                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n   298→                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n   299→                            return True\n   300→    return False\n   301→\n   302→\n   303→def _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n   304→    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n   305→    func = call.func\n   306→    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n   307→        return True\n   308→    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n   309→        return True\n   310→    return False\n   311→\n   312→\n   313→def analyze_unwired_callables(\n   314→    config: WiringConfig,\n   315→    source_dir: Path,\n   316→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   317→    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n   318→\n   319→    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n   320→    1. Parse all Python files, extract Optional[Callable] constructor params\n   321→    2. For each injectable, search all files for keyword call sites\n   322→    3. If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n   323→    4. Apply whitelist suppression\n   324→\n   325→    Args:\n   326→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   327→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   328→\n   329→    Returns:\n   330→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_callable\".\n   331→    \"\"\"\n   332→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   333→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   334→\n   335→    for f in files:\n   336→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   337→        if tree is not None:\n   338→            trees[f] = tree\n   339→\n   340→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   341→\n   342→    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n   343→        injectables = _extract_injectable_params(tree, str(file_path))\n   344→        for symbol, param_name, lineno in injectables:\n   345→            class_name = symbol.split(\".\")[0]\n   346→            if not _find_wiring_call_sites(param_name, class_name, trees):\n   347→                findings.append(\n   348→                    WiringFinding(\n   349→                        finding_type=\"unwired_callable\",\n   350→                        file_path=str(file_path),\n   351→                        symbol_name=symbol,\n   352→                        line_number=lineno,\n   353→                        detail=(\n   354→                            f\"Parameter '{param_name}' typed Optional[Callable] \"\n   355→                            f\"with default None is never wired by any call site\"\n   356→                        ),\n   357→                        severity=\"critical\",\n   358→                    )\n   359→                )\n   360→\n   361→    # Apply whitelist\n   362→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   363→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   364→\n   365→\n   366→# --- G-002: Orphan Module Analysis (section 5.2.2) ---\n   367→\n   368→\n   369→def _find_provider_dirs(source_dir: Path, provider_names: frozenset[str]) -> list[Path]:\n   370→    \"\"\"Find directories matching provider_dir_names convention.\"\"\"\n   371→    providers: list[Path] = []\n   372→    for d in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*\")):\n   373→        if d.is_dir() and d.name in provider_names:\n   374→            providers.append(d)\n   375→    return providers\n   376→\n   377→\n   378→def _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> set[str]:\n   379→    \"\"\"Extract all imported module/symbol names from an AST.\"\"\"\n   380→    imports: set[str] = set()\n   381→    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   382→        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n   383→            for alias in node.names:\n   384→                imports.add(alias.name)\n   385→        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n   386→            if node.module:\n   387→                imports.add(node.module)\n   388→                for alias in node.names:\n   389→                    imports.add(f\"{node.module}.{alias.name}\")\n   390→    return imports\n   391→\n   392→\n   393→def analyze_orphan_modules(\n   394→    config: WiringConfig,\n   395→    source_dir: Path,\n   396→    file_references: dict[str, list[str]] | None = None,\n   397→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   398→    \"\"\"Detect Python modules in provider directories with zero inbound imports.\n   399→\n   400→    Algorithm (section 5.2.2):\n   401→    1. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n   402→    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n   403→       the provider dir imports it\n   404→    3. If file_references provided (dual evidence rule), also check if\n   405→       any FileAnalysis.references mention the module — modules with\n   406→       references but no imports are NOT flagged as orphans\n   407→    4. If zero importers AND zero references, emit orphan_module finding\n   408→    5. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n   409→\n   410→    Args:\n   411→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   412→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   413→        file_references: Optional mapping of file_path -> list of references\n   414→            from FileAnalysis.references (populated by AST plugin). When\n   415→            provided, enables dual evidence rule. When None, falls back\n   416→            to import-graph-only evidence.\n   417→\n   418→    Returns:\n   419→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n   420→    \"\"\"\n   421→    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n   422→    if not provider_dirs:\n   423→        return []\n   424→\n   425→    # Collect all Python files and parse them for imports\n   426→    all_files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, [])\n   427→    all_imports: set[str] = set()\n   428→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   429→\n   430→    for f in all_files:\n   431→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   432→        if tree is not None:\n   433→            trees[f] = tree\n   434→\n   435→    # Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n   436→    for f, tree in trees.items():\n   437→        is_in_provider = any(\n   438→            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n   439→        )\n   440→        if not is_in_provider:\n   441→            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n   442→\n   443→    # Build aggregated reference set for dual evidence rule\n   444→    all_references: set[str] = set()\n   445→    if file_references is not None:\n   446→        for refs in file_references.values():\n   447→            all_references.update(refs)\n   448→\n   449→    dual_evidence_active = file_references is not None\n   450→\n   451→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   452→\n   453→    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n   454→        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n   455→            # Apply exclude patterns\n   456→            if any(fnmatch(py_file.name, pat) for pat in config.exclude_patterns):\n   457→                continue\n   458→\n   459→            # Derive the module path components\n   460→            try:\n   461→                rel = py_file.relative_to(source_dir)\n   462→            except ValueError:\n   463→                continue\n   464→\n   465→            # Build possible import names\n   466→            module_stem = py_file.stem\n   467→            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n   468→\n   469→            # Evidence 1: Check if any external file imports this module\n   470→            is_imported = False\n   471→            for imp in all_imports:\n   472→                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n   473→                    is_imported = True\n   474→                    break\n   475→\n   476→            if is_imported:\n   477→                continue\n   478→\n   479→            # Evidence 2 (dual evidence rule): Check FileAnalysis.references\n   480→            if dual_evidence_active:\n   481→                has_reference = False\n   482→                for ref in all_references:\n   483→                    if module_stem in ref or module_dotpath in ref:\n   484→                        has_reference = True\n   485→                        break\n   486→\n   487→                if has_reference:\n   488→                    # Module has references but no imports — dual evidence\n   489→                    # prevents false positive\n   490→                    continue\n   491→\n   492→            # Both evidence sources confirm: no imports AND no references\n   493→            evidence_note = (\n   494→                \" (dual evidence: import-graph + AST references)\"\n   495→                if dual_evidence_active\n   496→                else \" (import-graph only; AST plugin not loaded)\"\n   497→            )\n   498→\n   499→            findings.append(\n   500→                WiringFinding(\n   501→                    finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n   502→                    file_path=str(py_file),\n   503→                    symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n   504→                    line_number=1,\n   505→                    detail=(\n   506→                        f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n   507→                        f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n   508→                        f\"{evidence_note}\"\n   509→                    ),\n   510→                    severity=\"major\",\n   511→                )\n   512→            )\n   513→\n   514→    # Apply whitelist\n   515→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   516→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   517→\n   518→\n   519→# --- G-003: Registry Analysis (section 5.2.3) ---\n   520→\n   521→\n   522→def _matches_registry_pattern(\n   523→    name: str, patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...]\n   524→) -> bool:\n   525→    \"\"\"Check if a variable name matches any registry detection pattern.\"\"\"\n   526→    return any(p.match(name) for p in patterns)\n   527→\n   528→\n   529→def _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   530→    name: str, tree: ast.Module, all_imports: set[str]\n   531→) -> bool:\n   532→    \"\"\"Check if a name is resolvable: defined in module or importable.\"\"\"\n   533→    # Check module-level definitions\n   534→    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n   535→        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n   536→            if node.name == name:\n   537→                return True\n   538→        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n   539→            if node.name == name:\n   540→                return True\n   541→        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n   542→            for target in node.targets:\n   543→                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n   544→                    return True\n   545→\n   546→    # Check if importable\n   547→    if name in all_imports:\n   548→        return True\n   549→\n   550→    return False\n   551→\n   552→\n   553→def analyze_registries(\n   554→    config: WiringConfig,\n   555→    source_dir: Path,\n   556→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   557→    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n   558→\n   559→    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n   560→    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n   561→    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n   562→    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n   563→\n   564→    Args:\n   565→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   566→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   567→\n   568→    Returns:\n   569→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n   570→    \"\"\"\n   571→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   572→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   573→    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n   574→\n   575→    for f in files:\n   576→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   577→        if tree is not None:\n   578→            trees[f] = tree\n   579→            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n   580→\n   581→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   582→\n   583→    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n   584→        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n   585→\n   586→        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n   587→            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n   588→                continue\n   589→\n   590→            for target in node.targets:\n   591→                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n   592→                    continue\n   593→                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n   594→                    continue\n   595→\n   596→                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n   597→                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n   598→                    continue\n   599→\n   600→                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n   601→                    if val_node is None:\n   602→                        continue\n   603→\n   604→                    # Explicit None is allowed\n   605→                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n   606→                        continue\n   607→\n   608→                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n   609→                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n   610→                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   611→                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n   612→                        ):\n   613→                            key_repr = (\n   614→                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n   615→                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n   616→                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n   617→                            )\n   618→                            findings.append(\n   619→                                WiringFinding(\n   620→                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n   621→                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n   622→                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n   623→                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n   624→                                    detail=(\n   625→                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n   626→                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n   627→                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n   628→                                    ),\n   629→                                    severity=\"critical\",\n   630→                                )\n   631→                            )\n   632→\n   633→                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n   634→                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n   635→                        val_node.value, str\n   636→                    ):\n   637→                        ref = val_node.value\n   638→                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n   639→                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n   640→                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   641→                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n   642→                        ):\n   643→                            key_repr = (\n   644→                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n   645→                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n   646→                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n   647→                            )\n   648→                            findings.append(\n   649→                                WiringFinding(\n   650→                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n   651→                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n   652→                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n   653→                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n   654→                                    detail=(\n   655→                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n   656→                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n   657→                                        f\"string path '{ref}'\"\n   658→                                    ),\n   659→                                    severity=\"critical\",\n   660→                                )\n   661→                            )\n   662→\n   663→    # Apply whitelist\n   664→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   665→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   666→\n   667→\n   668→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   669→# Top-level entry point\n   670→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   671→\n   672→\n   673→def run_wiring_analysis(\n   674→    config: WiringConfig,\n   675→    source_dir: Path,\n   676→) -> WiringReport:\n   677→    \"\"\"Run all three wiring analyzers and produce a WiringReport.\n   678→\n   679→    Args:\n   680→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   681→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   682→\n   683→    Returns:\n   684→        WiringReport aggregating findings from all analyzers.\n   685→    \"\"\"\n   686→    start = time.monotonic()\n   687→\n   688→    _, skipped = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   689→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   690→    files_analyzed = len(files)\n   691→\n   692→    unwired = analyze_unwired_callables(config, source_dir)\n   693→    orphans = analyze_orphan_modules(config, source_dir)\n   694→    registries = analyze_registries(config, source_dir)\n   695→\n   696→    duration = time.monotonic() - start\n   697→\n   698→    return WiringReport(\n   699→        target_dir=str(source_dir),\n   700→        files_analyzed=files_analyzed,\n   701→        files_skipped=skipped,\n   702→        unwired_callables=unwired,\n   703→        orphan_modules=orphans,\n   704→        unwired_registries=registries,\n   705→        scan_duration_seconds=round(duration, 4),\n   706→        rollout_mode=config.rollout_mode,\n   707→    )\n   708→\n   709→\n   710→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   711→# Report emission (section 5.4)\n   712→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   713→\n   714→\n   715→def emit_report(report: WiringReport, output_path: Path) -> Path:\n   716→    \"\"\"Write a wiring verification report with YAML frontmatter and 7 Markdown sections.\n   717→\n   718→    Frontmatter contains 16 fields per section 5.6. String fields are serialized\n   719→    with yaml.safe_dump() to prevent YAML injection (section 5.4).\n   720→\n   721→    Args:\n   722→        report: Aggregated wiring analysis report.\n   723→        output_path: Destination file path.\n   724→\n   725→    Returns:\n   726→        The output_path after writing.\n   727→    \"\"\"\n   728→    # Compute severity counts from unsuppressed findings\n   729→    unsuppressed = report.unsuppressed_findings\n   730→    critical_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n   731→    major_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"major\")\n   732→    info_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"info\")\n   733→    suppressed_count = sum(1 for f in report.all_findings if f.suppressed)\n   734→\n   735→    # What’s in `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`?\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`\n\nHigh-level summary:\n- It defines many pure semantic check functions that validate generated roadmap artifacts.\n- It imports:\n  - `WIRING_GATE` from `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/audit/wiring_gate.py`\n  - `GateCriteria` and `SemanticCheck` from `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n- It defines module-level gate constants such as:\n  - `EXTRACT_GATE`\n  - `GENERATE_A_GATE`\n  - `GENERATE_B_GATE`\n  - `DIFF_GATE`\n  - `DEBATE_GATE`\n  - `SCORE_GATE`\n  - `MERGE_GATE`\n  - `TEST_STRATEGY_GATE`\n  - `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE`\n  - `ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE`\n  - `DEVIATION_ANALYSIS_GATE`\n  - `REMEDIATE_GATE`\n  - `CERTIFY_GATE`\n- It exposes `ALL_GATES`, which includes `\"wiring-verification\"` wired to `WIRING_GATE`.\n\nImportant detail: `roadmap/gates.py` does not define the `GateCriteria` dataclass itself. It uses the shared schema from:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n### GateCriteria dataclass definition\n\nDefined in:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GateCriteria:\n    \"\"\"Defines what constitutes a passing output for a pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]\n    min_lines: int\n    enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"\n    semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None\n```\n\n### SemanticCheck definition\n\nAlso defined in:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    \"\"\"Pure Python check applied to file content. No LLM invocation.\"\"\"\n\n    name: str\n    check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]\n    failure_message: str\n```\n\n### gate_passed() function signature and definition\n\nThis is not in `roadmap/gates.py`. It is defined in:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py`\n\nSignature:\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n```\n\nDefinition behavior:\n- `EXEMPT`: always passes\n- `LIGHT`: file must exist and be non-empty\n- `STANDARD`: plus min line count and required frontmatter fields\n- `STRICT`: plus all semantic checks must pass\n\nCore definition:\n\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n\n    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    \"\"\"\n    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n\n    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    if not output_file.exists():\n        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n\n    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n        return False, (\n            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n            f\"in {output_file}\"\n        )\n\n    if criteria.required_frontmatter_fields:\n        ok, reason = _check_frontmatter(\n            content, criteria.required_frontmatter_fields, output_file\n        )\n        if not ok:\n            return False, reason\n\n    if tier == \"STANDARD\":\n        return True, None\n\n    if criteria.semantic_checks:\n        for check in criteria.semantic_checks:\n            if not check.check_fn(content):\n                return (\n                    False,\n                    f\"Semantic check '{check.name}' failed: {check.failure_message}\",\n                )\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\n### Notable roadmap gate composition detail\n\n`roadmap/gates.py` includes the audit wiring gate in pipeline order:\n\n```python\nALL_GATES = [\n    (\"extract\", EXTRACT_GATE),\n    (\"generate-A\", GENERATE_A_GATE),\n    (\"generate-B\", GENERATE_B_GATE),\n    (\"diff\", DIFF_GATE),\n    (\"debate\", DEBATE_GATE),\n    (\"score\", SCORE_GATE),\n    (\"merge\", MERGE_GATE),\n    (\"anti-instinct\", ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE),\n    (\"test-strategy\", TEST_STRATEGY_GATE),\n    (\"spec-fidelity\", SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE),\n    (\"wiring-verification\", WIRING_GATE),\n    (\"deviation-analysis\", DEVIATION_ANALYSIS_GATE),\n    (\"remediate\", REMEDIATE_GATE),\n    (\"certify\", CERTIFY_GATE),\n]\n```\n\n## 3. What’s in `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`?\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/gates.py`\n\nHigh-level summary:\n- It defines many pure semantic check functions that validate generated roadmap artifacts.\n- It imports:\n  - `WIRING_GATE` from `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/audit/wiring_gate.py`\n  - `GateCriteria` and `SemanticCheck` from `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n- It defines module-level gate constants such as:\n  - `EXTRACT_GATE`\n  - `GENERATE_A_GATE`\n  - `GENERATE_B_GATE`\n  - `DIFF_GATE`\n  - `DEBATE_GATE`\n  - `SCORE_GATE`\n  - `MERGE_GATE`\n  - `TEST_STRATEGY_GATE`\n  - `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE`\n  - `ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE`\n  - `DEVIATION_ANALYSIS_GATE`\n  - `REMEDIATE_GATE`\n  - `CERTIFY_GATE`\n- It exposes `ALL_GATES`, which includes `\"wiring-verification\"` wired to `WIRING_GATE`.\n\nImportant detail: `roadmap/gates.py` does not define the `GateCriteria` dataclass itself. It uses the shared schema from:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n### GateCriteria dataclass definition\n\nDefined in:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GateCriteria:\n    \"\"\"Defines what constitutes a passing output for a pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]\n    min_lines: int\n    enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"\n    semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None\n```\n\n### SemanticCheck definition\n\nAlso defined in:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    \"\"\"Pure Python check applied to file content. No LLM invocation.\"\"\"\n\n    name: str\n    check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]\n    failure_message: str\n```\n\n### gate_passed() function signature and definition\n\nThis is not in `roadmap/gates.py`. It is defined in:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py`\n\nSignature:\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n```\n\nDefinition behavior:\n- `EXEMPT`: always passes\n- `LIGHT`: file must exist and be non-empty\n- `STANDARD`: plus min line count and required frontmatter fields\n- `STRICT`: plus all semantic checks must pass\n\nCore definition:\n\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n\n    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    \"\"\"\n    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n\n    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    if not output_file.exists():\n        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n\n    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n        return False, (\n            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n            f\"in {output_file}\"\n        )\n\n    if criteria.required_frontmatter_fields:\n        ok, reason = _check_frontmatter(\n            content, criteria.required_frontmatter_fields, output_file\n        )\n        if not ok:\n            return False, reason\n\n    if tier == \"STANDARD\":\n        return True, None\n\n    if criteria.semantic_checks:\n        for check in criteria.semantic_checks:\n            if not check.check_fn(content):\n                return (\n                    False,\n                    f\"Semantic check '{check.name}' failed: {check.failure_message}\",\n                )\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\n### Notable roadmap gate composition detail\n\n`roadmap/gates.py` includes the audit wiring gate in pipeline order:\n\n```python\nALL_GATES = [\n    (\"extract\", EXTRACT_GATE),\n    (\"generate-A\", GENERATE_A_GATE),\n    (\"generate-B\", GENERATE_B_GATE),\n    (\"diff\", DIFF_GATE),\n    (\"debate\", DEBATE_GATE),\n    (\"score\", SCORE_GATE),\n    (\"merge\", MERGE_GATE),\n    (\"anti-instinct\", ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE),\n    (\"test-strategy\", TEST_STRATEGY_GATE),\n    (\"spec-fidelity\", SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE),\n    (\"wiring-verification\", WIRING_GATE),\n    (\"deviation-analysis\", DEVIATION_ANALYSIS_GATE),\n    (\"remediate\", REMEDIATE_GATE),\n    (\"certify\", CERTIFY_GATE),\n]\n```\n\n## 3. \"\"\"\n\n    finding_type: Literal[\"unwired_callable\", \"orphan_module\", \"unwired_registry\"]\n    file_path: str\n    symbol_name: str\n    line_number: int\n    detail: str\n    severity: invariant: category sums == severity sums == total.\n    Blocking count is derived from rollout_mode per OQ-6.\n\n    Attributes:\n        target_dir: Root directory that was analyzed.\n        files_analyzed: Number of Python files successfully parsed.\n        files_skipped: Number of files excluded or unparseable (OQ-2).\n        unwired_callables: Findings from unwired callable analysis (G-001).\n        orphan_modules: Findings from orphan module analysis (G-002).\n        unwired_registries: Findings from registry analysis (G-003).\n        scan_duration_seconds: Wall-clock time of analysis run.\n        rollout_mode: Active rollout mode for blocking semantics.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    target_dir: str = \"\"\n    files_analyzed: int = 0\n    files_skipped: int = 0\n    unwired_callables: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    orphan_modules: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    unwired_registries: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    scan_duration_seconds: float = 0.0\n    rollout_mode: str = \"shadow\"\n\n    @property\n    def all_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n        \"\"\"All findings across all categories.\"\"\"\n        return self.unwired_callables + self.orphan_modules + self.unwired_registries\n\n    @property\n    def total_findings(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Total finding count (category sum invariant).\"\"\"\n        return len(self.all_findings)\n\n    @property\n    def unsuppressed_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n        \"\"\"Findings not suppressed by whitelist.\"\"\"\n        return [f for f in self.all_findings if not f.suppressed]\n\n    @property\n    def clean(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"True if zero unsuppressed findings regardless of rollout mode.\"\"\"\n        return len(self.unsuppressed_findings) == 0\n\n    def blocking_count(self, mode: str | None = None) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Count of findings that block the gate for the given rollout mode.\n\n        Args:\n            mode: Override rollout mode. Uses self.rollout_mode if None.\n\n        Returns:\n            Number of blocking findings per OQ-6:\n            - shadow: 0 (never blocks)\n            - soft: critical unsuppressed only\n            - full: critical + major unsuppressed\n        \"\"\"\n        effective_mode = mode or self.rollout_mode\n        unsuppressed = self.unsuppressed_findings\n\n        if effective_mode == \"shadow\":\n            return 0\n        elif effective_mode == \"soft\":\n            return sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n        else:  # full\n            return sum(\n                1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity in (\"critical\", \"major\")\n            )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Analyzers (sections 5.2.1, 5.2.2, 5.2.3)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _collect_python_files(\n    source_dir: Path,\n    exclude_patterns: list[str],\n) -> tuple[list[Path], int]:\n    \"\"\"Collect Python files from source_dir, applying exclude patterns.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (included files, skipped count).\n    \"\"\"\n    included: list[Path] = []\n    skipped = 0\n\n    for py_file in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*.py\")):\n        name = py_file.name\n        if any(fnmatch(name, pat) for pat in exclude_patterns):\n            skipped += 1\n            continue\n        included.append(py_file)\n\n    return included, skipped\n\n\ndef _safe_parse(file_path: Path) -> ast.Module | None:\n    \"\"\"Parse a Python file, returning None on SyntaxError (R2 mitigation).\"\"\"\n    try:\n        source = file_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        return ast.parse(source, filename=str(file_path))\n    except SyntaxError as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"SyntaxError parsing %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n    except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"Cannot read %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n\n\ndef _apply_whitelist(\n    findings: list[WiringFinding],\n    whitelist: list[WhitelistEntry],\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Mark findings as suppressed if they match a whitelist entry.\"\"\"\n    suppressed_symbols = {\n        (e.symbol, e.finding_type) for e in whitelist\n    }\n    for finding in findings:\n        if (finding.symbol_name, finding.finding_type) in suppressed_symbols:\n            finding.suppressed = True\n            finding.severity = \"info\"\n    return findings\n\n\n# --- G-001: Unwired Callable Analysis (section 5.2.1) ---\n\n\ndef _extract_injectable_params(\n    tree: ast.Module, file_path: str\n) -> list[tuple[str, str, int]]:\n    \"\"\"Extract Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n\n    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n    \"\"\"\n    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if not isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            continue\n\n        for item in node.body:\n            if not isinstance(item, ast.FunctionDef) or item.name != \"__init__\":\n                continue\n\n            for arg in item.args.args:\n                if arg.arg == \"self\":\n                    continue\n                annotation = arg.annotation\n                if annotation is None:\n                    continue\n\n                # Check for Optional[Callable] or Callable | None\n                if _is_optional_callable(annotation):\n                    # Verify default is None\n                    if _has_none_default(item, arg):\n                        symbol = f\"{node.name}.{arg.arg}\"\n                        injectables.append(\n                            (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n                        )\n\n    return injectables\n\n\ndef _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n            slice_val = annotation.slice\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                return True\n            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n                slice_val = annotation.slice\n                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n\n    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n            return True\n        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n            return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n    args = func_def.args\n    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n    all_args = args.args\n    defaults = args.defaults\n\n    if not defaults:\n        return False\n\n    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n        if arg is target_arg:\n            default_idx = i - offset\n            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n                default = defaults[default_idx]\n                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n    return False\n\n\ndef _find_wiring_call_sites(\n    param_name: str,\n    class_name: str,\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n    for tree in trees.values():\n        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                # Check keyword arguments\n                for kw in node.keywords:\n                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n                            return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n    func = call.func\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n        return True\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_unwired_callables(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n    1. Parse all Python files, extract Optional[Callable] constructor params\n    2. For each injectable, search all files for keyword call sites\n    3. If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n    4. Apply whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_callable\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        injectables = _extract_injectable_params(tree, str(file_path))\n        for symbol, param_name, lineno in injectables:\n            class_name = symbol.split(\".\")[0]\n            if not _find_wiring_call_sites(param_name, class_name, trees):\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"unwired_callable\",\n                        file_path=str(file_path),\n                        symbol_name=symbol,\n                        line_number=lineno,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Parameter '{param_name}' typed Optional[Callable] \"\n                            f\"with default None is never wired by any call site\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"critical\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-002: Orphan Module Analysis (section 5.2.2) ---\n\n\ndef _find_provider_dirs(source_dir: Path, provider_names: frozenset[str]) -> list[Path]:\n    \"\"\"Find directories matching provider_dir_names convention.\"\"\"\n    providers: list[Path] = []\n    for d in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*\")):\n        if d.is_dir() and d.name in provider_names:\n            providers.append(d)\n    return providers\n\n\ndef _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> set[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract all imported module/symbol names from an AST.\"\"\"\n    imports: set[str] = set()\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n            for alias in node.names:\n                imports.add(alias.name)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n            if node.module:\n                imports.add(node.module)\n                for alias in node.names:\n                    imports.add(f\"{node.module}.{alias.name}\")\n    return imports\n\n\ndef analyze_orphan_modules(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n    file_references: dict[str, list[str]] | None = None,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect Python modules in provider directories with zero inbound imports.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.2):\n    1. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n       the provider dir imports it\n    3. If file_references provided (dual evidence rule), also check if\n       any FileAnalysis.references mention the module — modules with\n       references but no imports are NOT flagged as orphans\n    4. If zero importers AND zero references, emit orphan_module finding\n    5. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n        file_references: Optional mapping of file_path -> list of references\n            from FileAnalysis.references (populated by AST plugin). When\n            provided, enables dual evidence rule. When None, falls back\n            to import-graph-only evidence.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n    \"\"\"\n    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n    if not provider_dirs:\n        return []\n\n    # Collect all Python files and parse them for imports\n    all_files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, [])\n    all_imports: set[str] = set()\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in all_files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    # Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n    for f, tree in trees.items():\n        is_in_provider = any(\n            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n        )\n        if not is_in_provider:\n            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n\n    # Build aggregated reference set for dual evidence rule\n    all_references: set[str] = set()\n    if file_references is not None:\n        for refs in file_references.values():\n            all_references.update(refs)\n\n    dual_evidence_active = file_references is not None\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n            # Apply exclude patterns\n            if any(fnmatch(py_file.name, pat) for pat in config.exclude_patterns):\n                continue\n\n            # Derive the module path components\n            try:\n                rel = py_file.relative_to(source_dir)\n            except ValueError:\n                continue\n\n            # Build possible import names\n            module_stem = py_file.stem\n            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n\n            # Evidence 1: Check if any external file imports this module\n            is_imported = False\n            for imp in all_imports:\n                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n                    is_imported = True\n                    break\n\n            if is_imported:\n                continue\n\n            # Evidence 2 (dual evidence rule): Check FileAnalysis.references\n            if dual_evidence_active:\n                has_reference = False\n                for ref in all_references:\n                    if module_stem in ref or module_dotpath in ref:\n                        has_reference = True\n                        break\n\n                if has_reference:\n                    # Module has references but no imports — dual evidence\n                    # prevents false positive\n                    continue\n\n            # Both evidence sources confirm: no imports AND no references\n            evidence_note = (\n                \" (dual evidence: import-graph + AST references)\"\n                if dual_evidence_active\n                else \" (import-graph only; AST plugin not loaded)\"\n            )\n\n            findings.append(\n                WiringFinding(\n                    finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n                    file_path=str(py_file),\n                    symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n                    line_number=1,\n                    detail=(\n                        f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n                        f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n                        f\"{evidence_note}\"\n                    ),\n                    severity=\"major\",\n                )\n            )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-003: Registry Analysis (section 5.2.3) ---\n\n\ndef _matches_registry_pattern(\n    name: str, patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a variable name matches any registry detection pattern.\"\"\"\n    return any(p.match(name) for p in patterns)\n\n\ndef _resolve_name_in_scope(\n    name: str, tree: ast.Module, all_imports: set[str]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a name is resolvable: defined in module or importable.\"\"\"\n    # Check module-level definitions\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n                    return True\n\n    # Check if importable\n    if name in all_imports:\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_registries(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n\n        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n                continue\n\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n                    continue\n                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n                    continue\n\n                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n                    continue\n\n                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n                    if val_node is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Explicit None is allowed\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n                        val_node.value, str\n                    ):\n                        ref = val_node.value\n                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"string path '{ref}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Top-level entry point\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_wiring_analysis(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> WiringReport:\n    \"\"\"Run all three wiring analyzers and produce a WiringReport.\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        WiringReport aggregating findings from all analyzers.\n    \"\"\"\n    start = time.monotonic()\n\n    _, skipped = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files_analyzed = len(files)\n\n    unwired = analyze_unwired_callables(config, source_dir)\n    orphans = analyze_orphan_modules(config, source_dir)\n    registries = analyze_registries(config, source_dir)\n\n    duration = time.monotonic() - start\n\n    return WiringReport(\n        target_dir=str(source_dir),\n        files_analyzed=files_analyzed,\n        files_skipped=skipped,\n        unwired_callables=unwired,\n        orphan_modules=orphans,\n        unwired_registries=registries,\n        scan_duration_seconds=round(duration, 4),\n        rollout_mode=config.rollout_mode,\n    )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Report emission (section 5.4)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef emit_report(report: WiringReport, output_path: Path) -> Path:\n    \"\"\"Write a wiring verification report with YAML frontmatter and 7 Markdown sections.\n\n    Frontmatter contains 16 fields per section 5.6. String fields are serialized\n    with yaml.safe_dump() to prevent YAML injection (section 5.4).\n\n    Args:\n        report: Aggregated wiring analysis report.\n        output_path: Destination file path.\n\n    Returns:\n        The output_path after writing.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Compute severity counts from unsuppressed findings\n    unsuppressed = report.unsuppressed_findings\n    critical_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n    major_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"major\")\n    info_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"info\")\n    suppressed_count = sum(1 for f in report.all_findings if f.suppressed)\n\n    # blocking_findings depends on rollout_mode\n    blocking = report.blocking_count()\n\n    # Build frontmatter dict (16 fields per section 5.6)\n    fm: dict = {\n        \"gate\": \"wiring-verification\",\n        \"target_dir\": report.target_dir,\n        \"files_analyzed\": report.files_analyzed,\n        \"files_skipped\": report.files_skipped,\n        \"rollout_mode\": report.rollout_mode,\n        \"analysis_complete\": True,\n        \"audit_artifacts_used\": 0,\n        \"unwired_callable_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"orphan_module_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"unwired_registry_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.unwired_registries if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"critical_count\": critical_count,\n        \"major_count\": major_count,\n        \"info_count\": info_count,\n        \"total_findings\": len(unsuppressed),\n        \"blocking_findings\": blocking,\n        \"whitelist_entries_applied\": suppressed_count,\n    }\n\n    # Serialize frontmatter with yaml.safe_dump for string safety\n    fm_yaml = yaml.safe_dump(fm, default_flow_style=False, sort_keys=False)\n\n    # Build Markdown body with 7 sections (section 5.4.1)\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    # 1. Summary\n    sections.append(\"## Summary\\n\")\n    sections.append(\n        f\"- **Target**: {report.target_dir}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Files analyzed**: {report.files_analyzed}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Files skipped**: {report.files_skipped}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Rollout mode**: {report.rollout_mode}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Total findings**: {len(unsuppressed)}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Blocking findings**: {blocking}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Scan duration**: {report.scan_duration_seconds:.4f}s\\n\"\n    )\n\n    # 2. Unwired Optional Callable Injections\n    sections.append(\"## Unwired Optional Callable Injections\\n\")\n    uc = [f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed]\n    if uc:\n        for f in uc:\n            sections.append(\n                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n            )\n    else:\n        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed unwired callable findings.\\n\")\n\n    # 3. Orphan Modules / Symbols\n    sections.append(\"## Orphan Modules / Symbols\\n\")\n    om = [f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed]\n    if om:\n        for f in om:\n            sections.append(\n                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n            )\n    else:\n        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed orphan module findings.\\n\")\n\n    # 4.
